<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#FF0000;font-size:14pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><img src="g2017031618513175242400.jpg" title="" alt="" style="width:183px;height:73px;"></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:16pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Earthstone Energy, Inc. Reports Fourth Quarter and <br />Full Year 2016 Results</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:16pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Woodlands, Texas, March 15, 2017 <font style="font-weight:normal;">&#8211; Earthstone Energy, Inc. (NYSE MKT: ESTE) (&#8220;Earthstone&#8221;, the &#8220;Company&#8221;, &#8220;we&#8221; or &#8220;us&#8221;), today announced financial and operating results for the three and twelve month periods ended December 31, 2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, the Company announced its estimated proved reserves as of December 31, 2016.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">For the fourth quarter of 2016, Earthstone reported a net loss attributable to common stockholders of $33.0 million, or $1.48 per diluted share, which included a pre-tax non-cash impairment charge (related to goodwill and oil and gas properties) of $24.3 million, and Adjusted EBITDAX<sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(1)</sup>, a non-GAAP financial measure, of $7.0 million.  For the year ended December 31, 2016, the Company reported a net loss attributable to common stockholders of $54.5 million, or $2.92 per diluted share, including a pre-tax non-cash impairment charge (related to goodwill and oil and gas properties) of $24.3 million, and Adjusted EBITDAX<sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(1)</sup>, a non-GAAP financial measure, of $16.3 million.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Fourth Quarter 2016 Results</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.62%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:13.2pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:3.62%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18pt;line-height:13.2pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18pt;line-height:13.2pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#x2022;</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;color:#000000;line-height:13.2pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:18pt;"><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">Average daily production of 4,685 barrels of oil equivalent per day (&#8220;Boepd&#8221;), an 18% increase compared to the third quarter of 2016 and </font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">a </font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">21</font><font style="font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;color:#000000;">% increase compared to the fourth quarter of 2015<sup style="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">(2)</sup></font></p></td></tr></table></div>

<p style="margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Impairments</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">During the year ended December 31, 2016, the Company recognized a non-cash impairment expense of $24.3 million, including $2.9 million related to its proved properties, $3.9 million related to its unproved properties, and $17.5 million related to goodwill.</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">2016 Year-End Proved Reserves &#8211; SEC Prices</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The Company&#8217;s estimated proved reserves at year-end 2016, which were prepared in accordance with Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;SEC&#8221;) guidelines by the independent reservoir engineering firm of Cawley, Gillespie &amp; Associates, Inc. (&#8220;CGA&#8221;), were approximately 12.1 million barrels of oil equivalent (&#8220;MMBoe&#8221;), 78% of which were proved developed and 59% of which were oil.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.25%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">SEC rules require that calculations of economically recoverable reserves use the unweighted average price on the first day of the month for the prior twelve month period.&nbsp;&nbsp;The resulting oil and natural gas prices used for the Company&#8217;s 2016 year-end reserve report, prior to adjusting for quality and basis differentials, were $42.75 per barrel and $2.48 per MMBtu, respectively.  Prices net of differentials were $39.41 per barrel and $2.27 per MMBtu.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:7.25%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Based on such prices, the Company&#8217;s estimated proved reserves by category as of December 31, 2016, are provided in the following table.</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">2016 Year-End Proved Reserves &#8211; Strip Prices</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">CGA also prepared estimates of the Company&#8217;s proved reserves at year-end 2016 using strip prices as of December 31, 2016, adjusted for differentials.&nbsp;&nbsp;Reference oil prices for the years 2017 through 2021 ranged from $56.19 per barrel to $56.21 per barrel and were held flat at $56.21 per barrel thereafter.  Reference natural gas prices for the years 2017 through 2021 ranged from $3.61 to $2.90 per MMBtu and were held flat at $2.90 MMBtu thereafter.  Differentials vary by field but overall were approximately $4.00 per barrel for oil and $0.30 per MMBtu for natural gas.  Based on such strip prices, our reserves were approximately 18.6 MMBoe, 57% of which were proved developed and 66% of which were oil.  Management believes the disclosure of estimated reserves using strip prices is useful in that it offers stockholders additional information about the quantity and value of our reserves under an alternative price scenario to that of SEC prices.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, management generally makes decisions based on estimated future prices as is customary in the industry.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Bold Energy III LLC &#8211; Transaction Update</font></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">As previously announced on November 8, 2016, Earthstone entered into a definitive agreement whereby it will acquire all of the outstanding membership interests of Bold Energy III LLC (the &#8220;Transaction&#8221;) in exchange for 36.1 million Class B Earthstone common shares.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Transaction has been structured in a manner known as an &#8220;Up-C&#8221; structure.  Stockholders of Earthstone and members of Bold are expected to own approximately 39% and 61%, respectively, of the combined company&#8217;s then outstanding Class A and Class B common stock on a combined and fully diluted basis.&nbsp;&nbsp;Management presently estimates the Transaction to close in late April 2017.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Management Comments</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Frank A. Lodzinski, President and Chief Executive Officer of Earthstone Energy, Inc., commented, &#8220;The fourth quarter of 2016 was a transformational period for our Company.&nbsp;&nbsp;We achieved meaningful production growth by completing our Eagle Ford inventory and participating in our first Wolfcamp A well in Howard County, Texas.&nbsp;&nbsp;In 2017, we plan to drill and complete 11 gross (4.4 net) Eagle Ford wells in southwestern Gonzales County, Texas.  Further, as previously announced in November 2016, the pending acquisition of Bold Energy will position the Company as an operator in the prolific Midland Basin of west Texas.  We are anxious to get the Bold transaction closed and fully demonstrate the potential of the acreage to the market.  We expect to start with a one rig program in late April 2017, and we are planning to mobilize a second rig in the fourth quarter of 2017 to further accelerate development of Bold&#8217;s assets. In anticipation of closing, we have already started the process to integrate the operations of both companies.&#8221;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Conference Call Details</font></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;text-indent:11.07%;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Earthstone is hosting a conference call on Thursday, March 16, 2017 at 11:00 a.m. Eastern, to discuss its fourth quarter and full year 2016 results and current operations.&nbsp;&nbsp;Investors and analysts are invited to participate in the call by dialing 877-407-8035 for domestic calls or 201-689-8035 for international calls, in both cases asking for the Earthstone conference call.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A replay of the call will be available on the Company&#8217;s website and by telephone until 11:59 p.m. Eastern (10:59 p.m. Central), Thursday, March 30, 2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;The number for the replay is 877-481-4010 for domestic calls or 919-882-2331 for international calls, using Conference ID:<font style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#FF0000;font-size:14pt;"> </font>10282.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;;font-style:normal;color:#auto;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">About Earthstone</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Earthstone Energy, Inc. is a growth-oriented independent oil and gas company engaged in developing and operating oil and gas properties through an active and diversified program that includes acquiring, drilling and developing undeveloped leases and asset and corporate acquisitions.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company&#8217;s primary assets are located in the Midland Basin of west Texas, the Eagle Ford trend of south Texas,<font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font>and the Williston Basin of North Dakota.&nbsp;&nbsp;Earthstone is traded on NYSE MKT under the symbol &#8220;ESTE.&#8221;  For more information, visit the Company&#8217;s website at <font style="color:#000000;">www.earthstoneenergy.com.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="text-decoration:underline;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></p>

Please call the SEC at 1-800-SEC-0330 or visit the SEC&#8217;s website for further information on its public reference room.  In addition, the documents filed with the SEC by Earthstone can be obtained free of charge from Earthstone&#8217;s website at www.earthstoneenergy.com or by contacting Earthstone by mail at 1400 Woodloch Forest Drive, Suite 300, The Woodlands, TX, 77380, or by telephone at 281-298-4246.</p>

<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU7"></a><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Earthstone Energy, Inc.</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><br /></font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Reconciliation of</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> GAAP to</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font><font style="font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><br />Unaudited</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The non-GAAP financial measures of Adjusted EBITDAX and PV-10, as calculated by us below, are intended to provide readers with meaningful information that supplements our financial statements prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). These disclosures may not be comparable to similarly titled measures used by other companies. Further, these non-GAAP measures should only be considered in conjunction with financial statements and disclosures prepared in accordance with GAAP and should not be considered in isolation or as a substitute for GAAP measures, such as net income or loss, operating income or loss, standardized measure of discounted future net cash flows or any other GAAP measure of financial position or results of operations.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_MON_1373442145"></a><a name="_MON_1373442158"></a><a name="_MON_1373442197"></a><a name="_MON_1373442465"></a><a name="_MON_1373442623"></a><a name="_MON_1373443675"></a><a name="_MON_1373461571"></a><a name="_MON_1373461597"></a><a name="_MON_1373461625"></a><a name="_MON_1373461652"></a><a name="_MON_1373461685"></a><a name="_MON_1373461723"></a><a name="_MON_1373461750"></a><a name="_MON_1373694593"></a><a name="_MON_1373712831"></a><a name="_MON_1373778887"></a><a name="_MON_1373789682"></a><a name="_MON_1373974507"></a><a name="_MON_1381146547"></a><a name="_MON_1381146786"></a><a name="_MON_1381153065"></a><a name="_MON_1381153086"></a><a name="_MON_1381556153"></a><a name="_MON_1381556191"></a><a name="_MON_1381575702"></a><a name="_MON_1381747850"></a><a name="_MON_1381832766"></a><a name="_MON_1381917093"></a><a name="_MON_1382160646"></a><a name="_MON_1390645189"></a><a name="_MON_1390915202"></a><a name="_MON_1390915216"></a><a name="_MON_1390915277"></a><a name="_MON_1390915298"></a><a name="_MON_1390915320"></a><a name="_MON_1390915361"></a><a name="_MON_1390915371"></a><a name="_MON_1390915468"></a><a name="_MON_1390991165"></a><a name="_MON_1392458738"></a><a name="_MON_1392731585"></a><a name="_MON_1392731604"></a><a name="_MON_1392793939"></a><a name="_MON_1373441960"></a><a name="_MON_1373442064"></a>I. Adjusted EBITDAX</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Adjusted EBITDAX is used as a supplemental financial measure by our management and by external users of our financial statements, such as investors, commercial banks and others, to assess our operating performance compared to that of other companies in our industry, without regard to financing methods, capital structure or historical costs basis.&nbsp;&nbsp;We define &#8220;Adjusted EBITDAX&#8221; as net income (loss) plus, when applicable, (gain) loss on sale of assets; accretion; <font style="color:#000000;">impairment expense;</font> d<font style="color:#000000;">epletion, depreciation and amortization; exploration expense; rig idle expense; interest expense; interest income; non-cash (gain) loss on derivatives; </font>non-cash stock compensation expense;<font style="color:#000000;"> and income tax expense (benefit).</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Our Adjusted EBITDAX should not be considered an alternative to net income (loss), operating income (loss), cash flow provided by (used in) operating activities or any other measure of financial performance or liquidity presented in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our Adjusted EBITDAX may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of another company because all companies may not calculate Adjusted EBITDAX in the same manner.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">&#160;</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">II. PV-10</p>
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:11pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">PV-10 is derived from the Standardized Measure of discounted future net cash flows, which is the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure.&nbsp;&nbsp;PV-10 is a computation of the Standardized Measure on a pre-tax basis.&nbsp;&nbsp;PV-10 is equal to the Standardized Measure at the applicable date, before deducting future income taxes, discounted at 10%.&nbsp;&nbsp;We believe that the presentation of PV-10 is relevant and useful to investors because it presents the discounted future net cash flows attributable to our estimated net proved reserves prior to taking into account future corporate income taxes, and it is a useful measure for evaluating the relative monetary significance of our oil and natural gas properties.&nbsp;&nbsp;Further, investors may utilize the measure as a basis for comparison of the relative size and value of our reserves to other companies.&nbsp;&nbsp;We use this measure when assessing the potential return on investment related to our oil and natural gas properties.&nbsp;&nbsp;PV-10, however, is not a substitute for the Standardized Measure.&nbsp;&nbsp;Our PV-10 measure and the Standardized Measure do not purport to present the fair value of our oil and natural gas reserves.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The following table provides a reconciliation of PV-10 of the Company&#8217;s estimated proved properties to the Standardized Measure (in thousands):</p>
